MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[Part VI—Sec. 4

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, Muthuselvan, born as a male child to MR. Puthiyavan, born on 18th March 1984, residing at
Thangamman Kovil Street, Kalkurichi, Palamadai Post, Tirunelveli. After the biological change due to an elaborate
sexual reassignment surgery she has been reared as a female (Reference Dr. V. Jayaraman,
MS.Mch.,MNAMS.,DIB.N.B.Phd.FICS) Kilpauk Medical College and Hospital, Chennai-600 010.
The Clinical Examination under the reference above also shows that, I Could be reared as a female.
Hence, I, Muthuselvan, shall henceforth be known as M. SELVIMANOJ PREM KUMAR.

Tirunelveli,

MUTHUSELVAN.

18th February 2014.
